Lee</a>   </span> <span class="a-declarative" data-action="cr-popup" data-cr-popup="{&quot;width&quot;:340,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;AmazonHelp&quot;,&quot;height&quot;:340}" style="display:inline;"></span><span class="a-color-secondary"> on November 11, 2013</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R3SH5GN8LXOP30" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Color Name: black<i class="a-icon a-icon-text-separator"></i></span><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold">     Verified Purchase   </span>      <div class="a-section">   Like other reviewers have mentioned, there're a few problems with this case:<br><br>1. It's not slim. In fact, it adds considerable bulk to the phone, but I guess with the bulk comes better drop protection.<br>2. The thickness of the case makes it hard to push the phone's On/Off button.<br>3. MicroSIM cutout. In the Amazon's product picture, there's no cut out for MicroSIM, but the case itself has the cutout. Useful for those who likes to change their SIM card every few days.<br>4. Glare from flash photography. The thickness and close proximity of the case to the flash causes some light to bounce back to the camera and results in glare in the pictures.<br><br>Caseology should do a few things: Fixed problems #3, #4 and leave out the word 'Slim' from the product name.<br><br>Oh, do not be fooled by the average 4.5+ rating of this product. Make sure you sort the review by 'Newest' and you will notice all the good reviews were for a different case (Nexus 4, etc). </div>  </div>             <a class="a-link-normal comment-link" title="4" It does appear the price on these has gone up, but that's really something to be expected as quality vs price before was almost too good.  Now, it's still a good value, but it's right around where the competition is -- good for you, Caseology!<br><br>At any rate, on to my initial impressions with this case (I ordered the leather hybrid one in white.)<br><br>Cutouts (4.5/5 stars): extremely impressed with the cutouts.  They're very precise and clean, and exactly where you want them - except one thing I find weird and dislike, but maybe you will not.  There is a cutout for the sim card! I dislike this because the sim card is NOT something you need to access often, and this case comes on/off very easily anyways (not falls off, but it can come off pretty easily if you want it to), so I really don't understand the need.  The thing I hate absolute most about this is that it severely diminishes the strength of the plastic above it(that borders the screen) and makes it easy to wiggle, push outward, etc.  If you just lightly push that piece it'll move.  I really, strongly dislike that.<br>Other than that, this is a 5/5 star category for me.<br><br>Looks: 4.5/5 stars.<br>The transition from the black around the sides to the white leather-like backing is quite smooth and looks great. However, if you look closely (or even from afar on the worst corner) the line has some unintended curvature to it.  I can best describe it as a subtle wave.</span><span class="a-declarative" data-action="columnbalancing-showfullreview" data-columnbalancing-showfullreview="{&quot;rest&quot;:&quot; It isn&#39;t that bad, except I do have one corner where it&#39;s most noticeable and I would&#39;ve recognized it even if I hadn&#39;t reviewed the case.&lt;br /&gt;I am absolutely in love with the leatherlike hybrid material on the back of this case. It&#39;s grippy, smooth, and has an EXCELLENT texture to it.  It&#39;s not a problem for me, but the texture is somewhat difficult to see (to differentiate between that material and just a normal plastic backing) unless you&#39;re observing the phone closely.  I also think the Caseology logo is quite big (too big), but it&#39;s a branding thing for a company I really like - no harm, no foul here.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Form factor (4.5/5 stars): I think this case has just about the right amount of protection here.  You want something that will protect your phone, but at the same time isn&#39;t a monster in terms of thickness (I&#39;m looking at you, Otterbox [&amp; many others]).  As long as you&#39;re not doing anything too crazy, this case will protect you so you don&#39;t need that kind of monster case. I feel like I&#39;d be just fine if this slipped out of my hand (or my notorious falls out of my lap and onto the pavement literally any time I am a passenger in a vehicle). After using my Nexus 5 for a day without a case, however, this does feel slightly bulky to me (it isn&#39;t, but it feels like that since I had nothing on it yesterday). I&#39;m likely going to fight having a case on this phone, as I think with the dimensions of the phone having any case makes it difficult to use with one hand.  It definitely feels just slightly too big with a case on. However, this is a great case and will most definitely be the case I use on this phone.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Price: 6/5 stars.  Honestly, I think Caseology really hits a home run with their products when you talk quality vs price.  Quality is superb, packing looks great, and you get a thank you that feels very sincere given how it&#39;s presented.  I feel like giving 4.5/5 stars on each category was harsh for such a nice product that comes for under $10.  I wasn&#39;t reviewing this like it was a cheap product.  I reviewed it like was the top of the line product and I&#39;m looking for things people should be aware of!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;These guys are just great, and I&#39;ll continue to use them always.  I&#39;m sure I&#39;ll end up ordering more Caseology Nexus 5 cases! :)&quot;}"><a class="a-link-normal" Triebold</a>   </span> <span class="a-declarative" data-action="cr-popup" data-cr-popup="{&quot;width&quot;:340,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;AmazonHelp&quot;,&quot;height&quot;:340}" style="display:inline;"></span><span class="a-color-secondary"> on November 6, 2013</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R2EZVXW71Y45J2" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-secondary">Color Name: Leather White<i class="a-icon a-icon-text-separator"></i></span><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold">     Verified Purchase   </span>      <div class="a-section">   I bought the white leather version of this case for my Nexus 5. It fits my Nexus 5 very well. It seems to provide a lot of protection with a minimal amount of thickness to the case. The camera lens on the Nexus 5 protrudes slightly beyond the back of the phone, and this case, which is about 2mm thick, raises the phone enough so that the lens no longer contacts the table when you set it down. The cutouts align very well with the buttons on the phone. Yes, there is a single, wide, cutout for the power button and the SIM card, but this may not be all bad. For one, it provides more clearance for your finger to get at the power button. I think that clearance would be awful small if the cutout were only big enough for the power button alone. Secondly, some people do change their SIM card often such as when traveling to another country, and this case will permit them to change the SIM card without removing the case.<br><br>I like the way the upper lip of the case extends slightly above the surface of the phone. This keeps the screen off the table when you place the phone face-down.<br><br>The leather grain pattern is very faint, so it doesn't really look like real leather. I think a more deeply-embossed grain pattern would be better.<br><br>This case does not interfere with the functionality of my Qi wireless charging pad.<br><br>Overall great value for a good-looking case that provides a lot of protection for my phone. </div>  </div>        <a class="a-link-normal comment-link" title="1"
